State Bit Width, Hash Bit Length, Number of 'a's in the Input, Time to completion H:MM:SS.FFFFF 
NOTE: the individual bytes in the arrays are all 0x61 (ASCII 'a'), this was done due to memory spikes from String
object overhead needlessly consuming GB of memory. The original times were gathered on an Intel i7 from a Surface
Pro 4 running Windows 10 and Visual Studio 2015.

So the first example is SKEIN256 with a 160 bit output length with input 'aa', resulting in a byte array of:
3B 90 60 28 AF 12 0D 2D 12 A0 AB 23 4A 12 C9 86 4D 4F 57 22 (which is displayed Base64 encoded for brevity)
